Enthusiastic Fundraising in Harbin

Various Parties Actively Participating, Hundreds of Thousands Already Raised

Total Mobilization of the Education Community, Unfortunate Tragedy Occurs

Municipal Government to Undertake a 150,000 Yuan Fundraising Campaign

Harbin Correspondence: People from all walks of life here have enthusiastically risen to the occasion to raise funds for the Jianghuai flood disaster. Those already underway include the fundraising by the Harbin Provincial Flood Relief Association, which plans to raise 200,000 yuan. The Bankers' Association has advanced 100,000 yuan, using 80,000 yuan to purchase grain to be transported to the disaster area and remitting 20,000 yuan to the Shanghai Relief Association for distribution. The Municipal Bureau of the Special City held a four-day fundraising fair from the 5th to the 8th of this month, raising over 30,000 yuan in cash, which will also be remitted to the disaster area in the coming days to be distributed by General Zhu Ziqiao. The Special District Education Commissioner Zhou Shouyi also ordered all primary and secondary school teachers and students in the district to mobilize on the 9th of this month to solicit donations from all parties, exerting their efforts for one day, achieving great results. However, an unfortunate tragedy occurred, which was truly unexpected. Prior to this, the Education Department had prepared for many days, printing donation booklets and distributing them according to the number of students and staff in each school. On that day, they were free to solicit donations from the public. Each secondary school student received a donation booklet and was required to fill it out, regardless of the amount of the donation. Primary school students received one booklet for every five students and were required to raise at least five jiao. Teachers and staff also received a donation booklet each to solicit donations. Therefore, on that day, the education community of the Special District, from the Commissioner to the laborers, mobilized, and the streets and trams were filled with male and female students soliciting donations. There are over 30,000 students in the Special District. By evening, the total amount raised was over 30,000 yuan, which was extremely satisfactory. Among them, Commissioner Zhou Shouyi personally raised over 2,000 yuan, and some laborers raised 20 to 30 yuan. The school with the best fundraising results was the District First Girls' Middle School, which raised over 4,000 yuan. The others also raised 2,000 to 3,000 yuan, or even 800 to 900 yuan. The individual with the best fundraising record was Yuan Xinglian, a student from the First Girls' Middle School, who raised 224 yuan. However, Gao Qinglan, a student from the ninth grade of junior high school at the school, was unfortunately hit by a No. 64 car while soliciting donations in Qinjiagang at 1:00 PM that afternoon. She suffered a fractured skull and died on the morning of the 10th. Gao was from Shandong and only 18 years old. Her parents are both alive. The education community is deeply saddened by her death. A memorial service is scheduled for the 13th. This is also an unfortunate incident in the charitable fundraising efforts in Harbin. It is reported that the Binjiang Municipal Preparatory Office has also joined forces with gentry merchants and various agencies in Daowai to hold a 150,000 yuan fundraising campaign. The plan has been finalized and is expected to be launched around the 15th. Once the funds are collected, they will be remitted to the disaster area through the Jilin Provincial Government, and the victims can expect another drop of sweet dew. (10th)

The Conspiracy of the Third International and Soviet Russia

(Continuation from the Previous Issue)

An Open Letter from the Standing Committee of the National Labor Union Discussing the International Labor Union Issue:

The theories of the Li Lisan faction are purely adventurist. The various struggles and strikes under Li's guidance were not sufficiently prepared in advance, and there was no understanding of the tactics of struggle. As for the various political slogans, they were also too mechanical, so the results were minimal. In the future, we must have a deep understanding of the characteristics of each struggle and have corresponding preparations and meticulous plans. There are still a few comrades at the lower levels who are deluded, thinking that Li Lisan's theories are based on a position of struggle, and that the theories we currently hold are for peaceful progress. This kind of misconception must be corrected (the best way is to publicly publish this text and the resolutions of the Fifth Congress). We must actively prepare to cope with the struggles that are about to break out in various factories, such as the struggles in silk factories, which are one example, because these struggles often occur during the plum rain season. We have sent a comrade to the silk factories to conduct a detailed investigation and encourage workers to make demands to the factory management (these demands should be immediately reported to the Standing Committee). The comrades responsible for various industries have also received considerable training, so that they have a deep understanding of the actual situation in each industry, so as to gradually realize our plan. There are about three million workers in China, but only two or three thousand of them are in contact with us, which proves that we still need to intensify our work and proves that we have been too indifferent to them in the past, so we are unable to lead various struggles. It is undeniable that we do not have a clear idea of how to start mass work. Therefore, we should immediately establish committees separately for various important industries, and we hope that the Central Committee will quickly send cadres to assist us. The comrades who will be sent to work in various places in the future should be given a mission to actively establish these committees wherever they go. We already have a comrade working in the Shanggang Iron Manufacturing Industry. As for Comrade He Zhongrong, he still has a task to go to Wuhu. When he returns to Shanghai in the future, he plans to be sent to work in the concession. After he leaves Shanghai, we have found a suitable comrade to replace his work. In short, the labor movement of our party under the leadership of Li Lisan is nothing more than armchair strategy. If we do not change our strategy immediately, it will inevitably become more difficult in the future. Within a week, we will give priority to establishing three committees for the textile, steel, and mining industries (the location of the mining committee is in Tianjin). However, there are no suitable comrades to be in charge of the textile industry, so for the time being, only the director of the Women's Department can temporarily act as its agent. We hope that the Central Committee can select one person from the fifteen students who have recently returned to China to take on this task. Recently, some lower-level comrades have believed that the organization of various committees from top to bottom does not meet the needs of reality, and some people believe that these affiliated organizations should only be given corresponding work within the scope of their name, so that they have independence. This kind of argument is not without merit, because in the past, these affiliated organizations have actually replaced the labor unions. In the past, when we recruited cadres, we always selected comrades from various factories and sent them to work elsewhere, thus often losing contact with the workers. Therefore, we should immediately change our methods. We plan to organize a training group. All comrades who are sent to work in factories must undergo this training. In the past, when we organized labor unions, the superior organs sent comrades to various factories and ordered them to do so, which was unavoidable. In the future, we should first send comrades to work among the masses, organize real labor unions, and be completely based on the workers' autonomy to conform to the spirit of democratic organization. We must intensify this work. We have already drafted a five-point plan and expect it to be approved within a day or two.

In the next week, we will discuss and review the plan for labor work in the Soviet area again, because in the past we have often ignored the yellow labor unions. If we do not study them in detail, we will have no way to understand their actual situation. When we discuss this issue, we should invite the comrades who are currently working in the yellow postal union and tram union to participate. At the same time, when we discuss other affiliated organizations, we must also invite the comrades who are related to those organizations to participate, so as to avoid alienation. Our most urgent task at present is to eliminate the erroneous ideas of the past about this kind of work, because from the perspective of the history of the party, it can be said that until today, the meaning of labor unions has not been clearly understood. In the past, right-wing forces were everywhere, and even now, there are still such people active. As a result, the party and the labor unions are almost in an antagonistic position, and in the past, comrades only obeyed the decisions of the superior organs and had no room for discussion, so it was also unavoidable. Regarding this issue, we will have a special article published in the "Worker" and conduct a public discussion of daily issues. The National Labor Union has adopted the ssoT draft and accepted the evaluation of the union's congress. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

A Record of the Inspection of the Seawall by Various Sectors: The Jinshanwei seawall has not been repaired for many years. Last month, strong winds and huge waves destroyed the second and third sections of the seawall, and the fourth and fifth sections are also in imminent danger. On the 13th, leaders from the Party, government, military, and business communities of Songjiang County, accompanied by Xue Xingbei, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau's Embankment Works Office, and technician Shen Baozhang, sailed there on a steamship at 7:00 AM. After arriving at the port, they jointly boarded the embankment to inspect it, examining each section in detail from east to west. The fifth section did not have any major dangers. The large yellow stones placed inside the wooden stakes of the fourth section were swept onto the embankment by huge waves, and the erosion of the mud posed a great danger. The third section is a cement project contracted by a construction factory in Shanghai and is not yet completed. This time, it was also destroyed by the waves. It is generally said that the designer of this section lacks engineering and physics knowledge. According to the old method of repairing embankments, wooden stakes are first driven in, spaced appropriately, and the middle is filled with stone blocks. Stone walls are then erected behind the stakes and covered with mud. When huge waves come, they are blocked by the stone blocks, and the water enters the stone holes, which is enough to disperse their force. This method is more complete. Now, with the cement wall standing on the seashore, when huge waves rush in, they will encounter an obstacle and their force will be stimulated to be even more violent. The project manager should find a way to improve it. It has been determined that the junction between the second section and the first section is the most dangerous because the mountains of Jinshan, Shoushan, and Minshan face each other overseas, and the tides are rapid, impacting the embankment with increasing intensity. Early repairs are necessary to avoid the autumn floods of the 18th of August. Subsequently, the merchants discussed the construction plan. In addition to the original 200 workers near the embankment, it is planned to recruit another 200 workers and have 200 soldiers dispatched from the Second Provincial Security Regiment, totaling 600 workers, to transport materials such as linen bags together to repair the embankment. The project is estimated to cost more than 34,000 yuan. In addition to borrowing 10,000 yuan from the road construction mu tax of this county, the remaining funds will be requested from the Construction Bureau by various sectors of the local community. Director Xue Xingbei will go to the province to collect them. After the inspection, they returned to the city. Sun Shiheng, a member of the Standing Committee of the County Executive Committee, will also report the inspection to the provincial department in detail and forward it to the Construction Bureau to quickly allocate funds for repairs to avoid danger.

Suzhou

Lake Bandits Kidnap and Murder: Donghetou Village, 12 miles from the town of Dongshan, was suddenly attacked at 2:00 AM yesterday (the 15th) by two bandit boats carrying more than 20 lake bandits armed with long and short firearms. They landed and swarmed into the home of Xu Yunfeng, looting for an hour, killing Xu's daughter-in-law, Guo, and kidnapping Xu Dingkui and a Ye surname mother and her two children. They stole a large amount of clothing, jewelry, and silver dollars. Afterwards, they took the stolen goods and headed south on Taihu Lake. The Eighth Water Police Team, upon hearing the news, dispatched a team to pursue and suppress them. Also, multiple bandit boats were discovered on the lake surface of Benji Village in Hengjing on the 14th, looting fishing boats. After the villagers reported it, the water police went to suppress them, and the bandits left. Chen Lin, the chief of the Eighth Public Security Branch in charge of the area, reported to the county government yesterday (the 15th) that bandit traces have been appearing in Hengjing since late August, causing public anxiety, and requested that the county government send a team to search and suppress them.

The Death of Zhang Li's Suspect: Zhang Li, a resident of Funing, outside Xumen, who was 59 years old, opened a fecal business in Suzhou. Several years ago, she recruited Li Mingkui as her son-in-law. However, because her son was abused to death, the relationship between Zhang and Li became strained. Meanwhile, Li had married Chen as his second wife, but still lived with Zhang. Yesterday (the 14th), Li Mingkui had an argument with Zhang Li over a minor matter. Yesterday morning (the 15th), Chen went out, and Li took his nine-year-old son and left. When Chen returned, she found Zhang Li had hanged herself in the room, and she had been dead for a long time. The ligature mark was very suspicious, and there was a wooden chair under her feet, higher than her feet. Neighbors were spreading rumors and discussing it. The local security officer has reported it to the local court for inspection.

Wuxi

Conflict Between Refugees and Villagers: Yesterday afternoon, more than a hundred male and female refugees from Mengcheng, Anhui, arrived at Chang'an Bridge in the northern district. Supporting the old and leading the young, they passed through Dongwang Village, taking vegetables from the fields, chickens and ducks from chicken coops and ponds along the way. At first, the villagers closed their doors to avoid them. But after the refugees left, they saw that the loss of vegetables and livestock was too great. So they beat gongs to gather a crowd and bravely pursued them. When they reached the end of the street in Chang'an Bridge, the two sides confronted each other, wielding wooden sticks and fighting. As a result, both sides were seriously injured. Shops in the town, fearing that they would be affected, quickly closed their doors and stopped business. They also telegraphed the County Public Security Bureau, requesting police to suppress the situation. Upon receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched twenty armed police officers to rush to the countryside. It was reported that the chiefs of the Anzhen Branch and the Bashiqiao Xia Branch had also received the report and sent police to rush there. But the refugees had already fled wounded to Bashiqiao. The town's merchant corps, together with the police, were fully armed to defend. The refugees did not dare to stay and went to Zhangjing Bridge.

Another Robbery Reported in the Countryside: At 11 o'clock the night before last, five or six bandits suddenly came to Zhou Heqing's house in Bashiqiao Town, which is under the county's jurisdiction. They climbed over the wall and entered the house, first tying up Heqing's son, Songshou, and then searching the room. Heqing heard the alarm and fled out the back door, beating a gong to call the police. The robbers hurriedly took the stolen goods and left. After checking, it was found that only clothes and jewelry worth more than ten yuan were stolen.

Banquet Donation Reduced to Contract Collection: The Wuxi Banquet Education Donation was implemented on January 1st of this year. Initially, Xu Gongdu contracted it for 2,400 yuan per month until the end of June, accumulating arrears of 7,000 to 8,000 yuan. Then the Finance Bureau directly collected it. But it was during the summer, and the collection did not improve. Recently, Qian Yinzai contracted it, with a monthly contract amount of 1,440 yuan. It was decided that it would be paid monthly starting in August. The Finance Bureau has commissioned it and is contacting restaurants and chefs in the surrounding villages to subcontract.

Hua Takes Over as Chief of the Public Security Bureau: Xu Jigui, the Chief of the County Public Security Bureau, was ordered to be transferred to Qingpu. The vacancy was filled by Hua Pu (Jianren), a local resident and current Captain of the 23rd Battalion of the 6th District of the Provincial Water Police, by order of the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Hu. After receiving the order, Mr. Hua took a train from Beijing to Wuxi on the 14th and went to the bureau at 8 o'clock yesterday morning to take over. After Xu handed over, he took a train from Wuxi to Shanghai and then went to Qingpu to take up his new post.

False Report of Robbery Case Opens for Trial: Guo Boxuan, the son of the late strongman Guo Zizhen, who lives in Guoxiang Lane, Bashiqiao, Sixth District (Tianxiashi) under the county's jurisdiction, is now a clerk in the Third Section of the Provincial Government. Last month, he returned home due to illness. He had a feud with Dai Ada, a resident of nearby Daixiang Lane. This time, when Dai Ada returned to Wuxi from Shanghai, Guo Boxuan lured him to his home to talk. Then he instigated Shen Jinbao and Zhao Longxing to tie Dai up with hemp rope. Then he rushed to the 12th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which has jurisdiction over the area, and falsely reported a robbery. The Chief of the Branch, Tan Weinan, immediately sent police to bring both parties to the bureau and send them to the headquarters. They were transferred to the County Court Procuratorate. After Prosecutor Du opened the court for questioning, he ordered Dai Ada to be temporarily detained. Guo Boxuan, Shen Jinbao, and Zhao Longxing were released on bail pending further investigation. Guo and others then found a shop guarantor at the Jinxing Garden Hotel at the entrance of Taiping Lane to bail them out.

Changzhou

Murder of Husband Case: The Main Culprit Arrested: Wu Agen, of Mengshu Village in the Sixth District of Wuyi, about five li from Dongheng Lin, was murdered with a knife and buried by his wife, Huang, and her lover, Shi Jingen, to cover up the crime. Recently, the eldest son of the deceased, Chunsheng, filed a complaint with the County Court. On the 14th, the Henglin Public Security Bureau arrested the murderer, Shi Jingen. According to the interrogation, he was 37 years old and from the same village as Wu Agen. He had been having an affair with Wu's wife, Huang, for three or four years. Agen worked in Shanghai and often quarreled with his wife when he came back. His wife had planned to murder him several times and had discussed it with him, but she couldn't find a way to do it. On June 28th of this year, Agen returned from Shanghai. At 2 pm on July 1st, his wife called him to his house. He saw Agen sleeping on a long bench, with his head resting on another square stool. He was sound asleep. At this time, two children were playing in the back village. Huang gave him a kitchen knife, and he chopped Agen on the left side of his head. He woke up, turned over, and wanted to resist. Huang stepped forward and held him down with a knife around his waist. Then he chopped Agen on the front of his head. Agen stopped breathing and died. Then Huang wrapped the body in a cotton robe, carried it to the sheep pen, covered it with grass, and wiped the blood stains on the door panel. He buried it in the field at midnight, etc. The Bureau Chief, Wang Quan, immediately recorded the confession and sent it to the City Public Security Bureau. On the 15th, he was transferred to the Court Procuratorate for interrogation.

Jingjiang

Taixing Bandit Arrested in Jingjiang: A wine merchant from Taixing was selling wine in Shanghai. He took 4,000 yuan and took a riverboat to Tianxing Bridge to land. The 25th Route Army stationed there came forward to inspect, and the foreign money was seen by the bandits. They followed for more than two li, strangled the wine merchant, and robbed the money. The local Public Security Bureau Water Police heard the news and searched everywhere. On the morning of the 12th, they were led to our county. They saw the bandit Chen Zuolin entering the West Gate. The police immediately pursued him. At the Shanhai Town inside the North Gate, Wang Fuxin, a post policeman, assisted in the capture. Wang's hand was bitten. After the bandit was captured, the county government interrogated him and immediately prepared a document and handed it over to the police to take him back to Taixing for legal action.

Impersonating Recruitment Officers Extorting in the Countryside: For several days, there have been people impersonating recruitment officers, extorting everywhere, and harassing good people in the countryside. On the 12th, Jiang Fuqing, Jiang Jinhong, and Ji Guifang were escorted by the 1st District and 2nd Branch Regiment. Wang Guomin, Liu Yubiao, Yao Desheng, and Yan Shidong were escorted by the 4th District Regiment Headquarters. County Chief Chen interrogated them, and the victims also came to court to question them. The soldiers are currently being detained pending a report to the provincial government for review.

Jiangyin

County Bureau Chiefs Request Exemption of Disaster-Stricken Land Tax: County Chief Peng and the Chief of the Finance Bureau reported that since Jiangyin has been hit by continuous wind and rain disasters, more than 300,000 mu of land have been without harvest, and more than 10,000 people are homeless, without clothes or food. In addition to distributing 5,000 yuan for emergency relief, it is still not enough. The other day, in accordance with the newly promulgated methods for surveying and reporting disasters, they telegraphed the provincial government, requesting that a commissioner be sent to the countryside to conduct a reassessment and exempt the land tax to benefit the disaster victims.

Nanjing Principal Issue Awaiting Resolution by the Education Department: The students of Nanjing Middle School launched a storm to drive out the principal, Zhang Zhongyou. Zhang left the school and went to the provincial capital to ask the Education Department for instructions. The school's board of directors also held a meeting in the capital on the 13th to discuss the principal issue. As a result, they will wait for the Education Department to resolve it. Before the Education Department resolves it, a committee organized by teachers and staff will maintain school affairs.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Provincial Government Raises Clothes for Disaster Victims: The Jiangsu Provincial Government telegraphed the county chiefs of each county yesterday, saying that this year, the disaster-stricken areas in the province are almost nine out of ten. The counties along the canal are especially tragic. The provincial government has been actively preparing and implementing the reception and relief efforts. However, as the deep autumn is approaching and the severe cold is coming, the issue of clothing for the disaster victims should also be prepared in advance. In addition to telegraphed requests to the Commander-in-Chief and Deputy Commander-in-Chief, and orders to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Security Department, the used clothes of the military and police should be allocated to the provincial government as soon as possible and transferred to the Relief Association for distribution. The county chief is urgently ordered to immediately announce to all sectors that anyone who has stored used clothes for men and women, young and old, single cotton, silk, and cloth, should donate them as much as possible and hand them over to the county government for transfer to the provincial government, so that they can be transferred to the Zhen Association for distribution and distribution, and they should be informed to the township heads and deputies in each district and town, and they should be responsible for soliciting donations to ensure that the people affected by the disaster can obtain cold-proof equipment.

Grain Circulation Allowed Within Jiangsu Province: The Jiangsu Province has suffered from severe flooding, and each county feels a lack of grain. Recently, local people in Jiangning, Yizheng, Liuhe, and other counties have gathered to discuss the prohibition of the transport of grain outside the county. After the county governments and others submitted their opinions to the provincial government, it was heard that the provincial government had instructed the counties that grain in accordance with the regulations should be allowed to circulate within the province. Grain merchants are allowed to circulate if they sell grain within the province, and the county is ordered to investigate and handle the matter properly, so as to take both into account.

Relief Association Requests to Dredge Disaster Victims: The Temporary Relief Association for the Flood in Northern Jiangsu said that a number of disaster victims from Northern Jiangsu arrive in Zhenjiang every day, and nearly a thousand of them stay. The Zhenjiang reception centers are full and there is no room for more. If more are transported in, regardless of how many, they will have to sleep in the open. If no measures are taken to dredge them, it will be difficult to receive them. Therefore, the chairman Ye was telegraphed yesterday, requesting that more reception centers be set up in the counties along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to dredge them separately. The county chiefs of each county were also telegraphed, instructing them to properly arrange and transfer the disaster victims when they arrive by truck in Zhenjiang. The Relief Association also telegraphed the county chiefs of Rugao and Taixing, saying that there are many disaster victims in Xingdong and other places, and they cannot go out to make a living without ships. Please send more tugboats to transport them nearby to Shanghai, Changzhou, Wuxi, and other places to find food.

Pinghu

Bandits Found in Dacheng Village: The bandit leader Qing Taibao Ashu of Dongxiang has been executed for a long time, but small groups of bandits are still hiding in various places. In addition, more than forty mutinied soldiers from the Sixteenth Regiment have not been captured and are mixed in among them. Robberies in the surrounding villages are frequent. At midnight the other day, more than thirty bandits suddenly came to the house of Chen Peisheng, a wealthy household in Dacheng Village. They intended to break in. Chen woke up in shock, quickly grabbed the gun he had prepared, climbed onto the roof, and beat a gong to call the police. The neighbors responded to the sound and gathered the villagers to rescue him. Seeing that the situation was not good, the thieves fled.

Hangping Highway Actively Under Construction: Although the road surface of the Zha Ping section of the Hangping Highway has been completed, the bridges have not yet been built, so it has not yet been opened to traffic. Now the Highway Management Office has sent a large number of workers to the Hongni Weir, the central receiving point of the Pingzha branch road. After surveying, it is planned to build five bridges: Yangshugang Bridge, Gaoqiao Bridge, Beihong Bridge, Beihelou Bridge, and Xinqiao Bridge. They are now trying to estimate the cost of construction in order to actively construct them.

Hangzhou

Jealousy Leads to Assault with Three Knife Wounds: Jiao Xiaohe, a resident of Lirenbang Lane in Hangzhou, works as a waiter in the Yanbinlou restaurant. His wife, Zhang, is 24 years old and beautiful, but she has as many as four lovers. At about 9 pm on the 14th, one of her lovers, Yang Yougen, suddenly went to her house with a sharp knife due to jealousy and stabbed the woman three times. She bled profusely and was seriously injured. The neighbors quickly reported to the police station, and the police rushed to the scene. The murderer had already escaped. The injured person was carried to the hospital for treatment.

Children in Sandun Rob and Murder for Money: The son of Jin Shou, a butcher in Wulitang, Sandun Town, Hangzhou County, was studying at the Fourth Elementary School in the town. The other day afternoon, the son of Jiang, who runs a tea shop in Xinshi, lured him to Sangang Road under the pretext of catching crickets. He snatched the gold ring from Jin's ear and tried to escape. Jin's child called for help, and Jiang pushed Jin's child into the pond, causing him to drown. His body floated to the surface of the water in the evening. Jin Shou was notified and recovered the body. Seeing that the gold ring was missing, he suspected that he had been murdered. Then he found out that Jiang's child had done it and had already fled to Xinshi. Yesterday, the Sandun Security Corps sent members to Xinshi to arrest the murderer and take him back to Sandun for trial in court.

First Lottery for Old Debt Bonds: The first lottery for the redemption of the old debt bonds of Zhejiang Province was held today (15th) by Tang Shijian, the Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Department of Finance, at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Representatives from various departments of the Provincial Government and various groups attended the meeting to supervise. This time, a total of 240,000 yuan of principal and 300,000 yuan of interest will be redeemed. A total of four prizes were drawn. Those whose last two characters on the face of the bond are the same as the winning number will be entitled to redeem the principal. The redemption will begin on the first of next month by the two Chinese local banks and the county governments. The winning numbers are as follows: 15, 33, 68, 85.

Ningbo

All Sectors Plan to Raise 100,000 Yuan for Disaster Relief: The Yin County Emergency Relief Committee for the Flood Disasters in Various Provinces convened a fundraising committee at 3 pm yesterday. Zhang Lanting, Jin Zhenxiang, Jiang Jieqing, Chen Nanqin, Zhao Bin, Xie Fengming, and dozens of others attended. They discussed fundraising methods and resolved: (1) The fundraising target is 100,000 yuan; (2) The fundraising period is limited to 15 days, with one payment every five days; (3) Fundraising methods: The committee will print donation books and distribute them to each member for fundraising; (4) Various industries and partners will voluntarily donate. The committee will send letters to various trade associations to convene meetings and forward letters to various shops for fundraising; (5) Various agencies, schools, and groups will be contacted by the committee members Chen Nanqin and Chen Ruxin.

Bandit Chen Xiao Zeng Executed by Firing Squad: Chen Xiaozeng, also known as Chen Jinbiao, from Yuyao, repeatedly gathered bandits in the Yuanjia Lane area to carry out arson and robbery. After the Self-Defense Corps learned of this, they reported to the County Security Corps for joint arrest. Chen Xiaozeng was arrested in a temple in Lianda Village and sent to the county for investigation. After the trial officer investigated, the suspect confessed. Therefore, a request was submitted to the province for approval. Yesterday, a secret order was received from the Zhejiang Higher Court, stating that since the suspect Chen Xiaozeng had confessed during interrogation, he should be sentenced to death. Therefore, yesterday, the Security Corps escorted the suspect to the execution ground and executed him by firing squad.

Hefei

Dingyuan Telegrams for Joint Attack on Communist Bandits: On the 27th of last month, a large number of communist bandits approached Dingyuan County, 120 li from Hefei. County Chief Zhang Yuanqun mobilized the county's security corps and fought fiercely with the communist bandits for two days and nights. They broke through the bandit dens in Zao Xiangmiao, Lujia Gang, and Wu Jiawei, killing the bandit leader Dai Guoxing and many other bandits. The communist bandits retreated to the junction of Shou, Ding, and He and entrenched themselves in an attempt to make a comeback. The County Chief telegraphed the General Headquarters and the Provincial Government for assistance. The Provincial Government sent the First Battalion of the Special Service Regiment, which arrived in Dingyuan on the 2nd. They are now opening to the southwest countryside to assist in the suppression. The telegram requested the Hefei County Government to block and suppress them. The acting County Chief ordered the district regiments of the northeast, four, five, and north, and two villages to strictly guard against them on the 6th.

31 to 18

The Southeast Jinan Liangjiang Triangular Women's Basketball Tournament, Southeast defeated Jinan by a landslide of 31 to 18 in the first game last night and won the final, Referee Shao Ji.

At the end, forward Chen Yuzhi suddenly fell ill and left the field. Situ Wei retreated to the guard position to monitor Pan Yueying, but she could not reverse the decline.

Decathlon Promotes Zhong Lianji

Yesterday was the second day of the All-Around Sports, and only the second half of the Decathlon was held. Therefore, the track and field was still deserted. Fortunately, there were staff and athletes in the national martial arts competition, as well as male and female visitors, which created a lively atmosphere. Unfortunately, the weather was not good. After the high hurdle competition of the Decathlon was over, when the discus was just beginning, the rain poured down and continued for about half an hour. The general competitors, referees, athletes, and boy scouts were all turned into drowned chickens. They had no choice but to announce a stop to the competition. So, they all looked for places to hide from the rain. In a short time, the podium and the athletes' rest area were crowded. In less than twenty minutes, a lot of water accumulated on the track and in the competition field. Fortunately, the floating clouds blew over and stopped at two o'clock. With an order, the boy scouts and the small two on the field responded to each other and led the way in the water diversion movement. In a short time, there was no drop of water on the track, so the competition continued. But several inches of water had accumulated in the competition field, so the second half of the Decathlon was not good yesterday.

Criticism of the Second Half of the Decathlon

Except for the high hurdles, the rest of the second half of the Decathlon held yesterday were affected by the rain, and the results were not good. Luo Dexian was originally expected to compete with Zhong, but he lost a lot of points in the pole vault and javelin events, totaling more than 90 points. In the future, it is hoped that Luo will work hard on the sports events in which the results are not good. Zhong's discus and 1,500 meters should also be practiced more often in the future. Otherwise, it will be difficult to compete with Zhang Lingjia of Liaoning and other Decathlon athletes from Beiping and other places for the championship in the future national games. Liang Jun became a good material for the long jump and triple jump. In the future, he should focus on training and not be greedy for more, so that the results of a single event will not improve much. Therefore, he should give up practicing the Decathlon.

Preliminary Round of National Arts Competition

The municipal sports meet's national arts competition held its opening ceremony yesterday afternoon around 1 PM. Those in attendance included Chu Minyi, Wu Jianquan, Tong Zhongyi, Wu Huichuan, Ye Dami, Lao Boshi, Liu Desheng, and referees Ye Liang, Chen Xuliang, Ma Yueliang, etc. The ceremony was carried out according to protocol. First, Chen Jiaxuan, chairman of the National Arts Department, informed all members of the rules and points of attention, as well as the attitude that athletes should adopt. Next, Chu Minyi delivered an instructional speech, encouraging everyone to strive for progress and win honor for the national arts community. Immediately after, he announced the start of the combat competition. Just as one group finished competing, a heavy rain suddenly arrived, and the people in the field rushed to the command post and basketball room to take shelter. Even the mat shed, which was less than ten feet in size, sheltered more than thirty people. Most of them were soaked through, resembling drowned chickens. At 3 PM, the rain stopped, and the competition resumed. However, the arena was slippery after the rain, causing competitor Cao Zufa to fall and slightly injure his arm. In total, six groups of men's lightweight class, two groups of light-middleweight class, and one group of women's class, totaling nine groups, competed. The results are as follows:

Men

(Lightweight Class) Group 1: Si Wang Xijie wins; Yi Wu Weng Sheng wins.

(Lightweight Class) Group 3: San Yi Chen Zhenyi wins; Si Ba Song Baomao wins.

On this day, the fighting style of the first group in the competition was relatively poor, but from the second group onwards, the performance gradually improved, becoming even better towards the end. Both sides used fists and legs, mostly legally. In particular, Liu Fengming with number 47, Gu Muchan with number 6, and Chen Zhenyi with number 31 were the best. As for Song Baomao with number 48 and Wei Hanming with number 5, although they unfortunately did not win, their body techniques and striking techniques were flawless. The women's group had good striking techniques, but their strength was not sustained, so the referees had to slightly shorten the time. After stepping down from the arena, reporters from various newspapers competed to take photos of them. As for the athletes, they were all able to obey the order and follow the rules, which was especially commendable. It is fortunate for the future of national arts.

Furthermore, due to the rain yesterday, some competitors withdrew from the competition. It is now scheduled to continue the competition starting at 1 PM this afternoon. Those who did not compete yesterday are expected to arrive by 12 noon. If they do not appear today, their participation will be considered a forfeit. Please take note.

5,000-Meter Race Walking Performance: Shi Jinsheng First

Since winning the Shanghai International Race Walking Championship, practicing race walking has become a popular trend. Furthermore, under the guidance of Shi Junyouhui, the organization of the Race Walking Association has been well-structured, and practice has been consistent and methodical, resulting in rapid progress. Yesterday, the result of the 5,000-meter performance at the track and field was that Shi Jinsheng won first place with a time of 26 minutes, 32 and 2/5 seconds. Looking at Shi's posture, it was unified from beginning to end, which was quite impressive. Compared to his posture in the previous two International Race Walking events, it has improved significantly. The postures of Zhang Zaojiu in second place and Hou Genren in third place were also quite good, but their thigh muscles were not as strong as Shi Jinsheng's, so their pace rate was slower. Xie Xingdao in fourth place had very small steps, and although his speed was extremely fast, it ultimately felt disadvantageous. The four people who achieved positions were all veterans of the Chinese race walking team. It is hoped that everyone will continue to work hard, not only to have a good performance at the National Games, but also to maintain the championship at this year's International Race Walking and win glory for China. The rankings and results of yesterday's performance are as follows:

First: Shi Jinsheng

National Record Set in Men's and Women's Swimming, Day 2, 200m Breaststroke Finals

Created by Ling Chongju, time: 3 minutes, 27 and 8/10 seconds.

Original national record held by Ma Zhihui, time: 3 minutes, 28 seconds.

The municipal sports meet swimming competition continued last night at the Jiaotong University swimming pool. The athletes were all in high spirits due to the finals, seeking the final victory. Therefore, the competition in each event was more intense than the previous day, attracting hundreds of spectators in the entire venue, who stretched their necks and watched with great interest. Among them, the 200-meter breaststroke was the most exciting. When the announcer reported the results of this event, the sound of cheers from the entire venue shook the building, as Ling Chongju had set a new national record. The competition situation is attached as follows:

(1) Competition Overview

Men's and Women's 50-meter Freestyle: The first event on the order list was the 50-meter freestyle competition. From the start to the end, Yin Yanjun and Lian Xiannan competed for first place, swimming side by side. At the final point, the two were only inches apart, but Yin Yanjun ultimately took the lead.

200-meter Breaststroke: One of the most exciting events of the night. Five splashes of water scattered, and only five human frogs could be seen bravely advancing. At the 150-meter mark, the top two were less than three meters apart. By the time they reached the finish line, Ling Chongxue had surpassed Yu Rongji by more than 25 meters, and Ling's posture was perfect, creating a new national record, which is truly a celebratory event.

Women's 100-meter Breaststroke: Ms. Gong Xiji performed a solo act, which was a unique scene in the competition.

Diving: Yu Rongji and Zhou Xuanguang were the best. Each jump and leap was full of tricks and looked very interesting. As a result of the competition, Yu won one point more than Zhou.

1,500-meter Freestyle: In this event, when turning after the 25-meter mark, the top two pushed forward at the same time, and the competition was extremely fierce. As a result, Lin Chaoyuan took the lead, followed by Chen Yuquan. When they reached the finish line, the two were only five inches apart.

100-meter Freestyle: Lian Xiannan and Yin Yanjun chased each other, advancing side by side. Yin passed Lian in the last lap. Although Lian was good at using the turn, he was ultimately defeated by Yin's remaining energy in the last few seconds.

Minxin Hero

Zhang Xiangqing defeats Situ Guang

Sets a new national record in the triple jump

Outperforms Wang Jihuai in the long jump

Fuzhou News Agency reports that the Fujian preliminary round for the National Games is actively being planned and carried out. The Sports Association, in order to select outstanding talents from the Fuzhou people to prepare for participation in the preliminary round, held a public sports meet at the Provincial Public Sports Field. Schools, groups, or individuals who participated were quite enthusiastic. Cheng Shizhui, Director of Education, also personally guided the event, and the sports results were very good. Zhang Xiangqing achieved a high jump result of 1.60 meters and a long jump result of 6.66 meters, outperforming Wang Jihuai, who had the best long jump result this year (Wang Jun jumped 6.64 meters at the Jiangnan University sports meet, which was the best result of the year). His high and low hurdles results were also good. His triple jump even broke the national record of 13.73 meters held by Situ Guang with a record of 14 meters, attracting attention from all walks of life. Zhang is from Longxi, Fujian, and studied at Waseda University in Japan. He usually works hard on sports training. When the university held sports events in Japan, he ranked second individually. This year, Zhang will represent Fujian in the National Games and will surely bring glory to Fujian.

The Back Waves Urge the Front Waves: A Record of the Ups and Downs of Dongda Athletes in Recent Years

(Shenyang Correspondence) Since the 14th North China Games of that year, Northeastern University has leaped to become the leader of domestic track and field. In the past three years, its glory has been brilliant, shining throughout China. It has consistently and steadily won championships in various competitions, both large and small, with its substantial strength. However, during this period, meritorious officials retired after achieving fame, and new talents emerged to the forefront. Several generations of back waves pushed the front waves, and the overall situation has undergone several ups and downs.

Sprints: In the North China campaign of that year, the main sprinter was Mr. Liu Changchun. Mr. Liu is still holding his position, but unfortunately, his strength may not be as good as before. Later, Dongte Teng Ruilin (who won the first place in the North China Junior 100m and 200m) transferred in, and then it developed even better. I remember once, Mr. Liu won first place with 10.8 seconds (in an ordinary small sports meeting), while Teng won second place with 11.1 seconds, which can be said to be rare. However, later, at the National Games, Teng was completely defeated due to lack of practice, and Liu also regressed due to a leg injury.

In the summer of the 19th year, Teng dropped out of school. At the same time, Mr. Li Yuezhou transferred in again. Li is a sprint expert, so he made up for Teng's vacancy. In the same year, in the Four Provinces Joint Games, he only lost to the "Flying General" by one step in the 100m race.

However, things change rapidly. Li also dropped out of school this summer, presumably to graduate. It is said that he is now working in the Tianjin military. At this time, Wu Jingyao, a leader in the North China junior sprints, was admitted. Mr. Wu has excellent physical fitness and will be able to achieve great accomplishments in the future.

Middle Distance: As for the middle distance, it was mainly led by Jiang Yunlong and Wang Xuanji in the early years, supplemented by Xue Yuxiang and Pang Shirong. At that time, at the North China Games, Wang won the 800m championship, and Jiang Yunlong, Chen Fengsheng, Xue and Pang monopolized the 1500m and won the beautiful name of the Four Horsemen. Before long, Chen Fengsheng dropped out of school first, followed by Pang, who also dropped out of school last year. Wang Xuanji's heyday has passed. Emerging players such as Wang Mingshen, Yu Xiwei, Wang Shaoye, Ma Degang, Zhang Baoxiang, and Liu Guxue have all surpassed him. So, Wang fell to become a 400m runner, and then fell to become a 200m runner. Xue Yuxiang unfortunately suffered from tonsillitis at the beginning of this year and rested for about a quarter. During the summer vacation, he unfortunately suffered from a leg disease again. He has been plagued by illnesses many times, and his ambition has been exhausted.

Long Distance: In the early years, the main long-distance runner was Jiang Yunlong. Jiang won the first place in the 1500m, 5000m, and 10000m at the North China Games. However, the 10000m was not his specialty, so after Zhao Dexin (also known as Zhao Mingsan) from Dalian came to the school, Jiang withdrew from the top spot in the 10000m and gave way to him. (In the National Games the following year, Zhao showed his power and made the people of the country deeply recognize the "Old Zhao" of the Northeast. However, unfortunately, Heaven was jealous of talent. When Old Zhao was ambitious and ready to go to Shanghai (to participate in the Far Eastern Games), he suffered a sudden illness due to participating in a 17-mile marathon. So, he watched others set off for the meeting, while he was trapped in illness for more than two months. By the time he recovered, he was as thin as firewood and dared not think about sports again in this life. Looking back on the past, it was nothing more than a heroic dream.

After Zhao retired, there was a lack of talent in the Northeast for a time. Therefore, in the Four Provinces Joint Games of that year, Liu Guxue of Dongte took advantage of the opportunity. However, unexpectedly, in the winter of that year, Liu Guxue also drifted into Dongda University, where everyone hopes. So, the long-distance world of Dongda was restored, and now Zhang Yongming has made considerable progress. It is expected that he will become a master soon.

Hurdles: As for the hurdles, there is no major change. The high hurdles are still Xiao Dinghua's specialty, but Zhang Lingjia is not willing to stay behind forever, and there has been a fierce competition recently. Also, the low hurdles have been changed to middle hurdles, so recently, there are many speculators who are committed to this item.

Jumping: In the early years, Xiao Dinghua was regarded as the leader of the jumping world, so he was also known as the Flying Grasshopper. But after the North China Games, Chuan Baorui from Dalian transferred in. This gentleman is tall and strong, and the three jumps (high jump, long jump, triple jump) are all his strengths. Now, except for the triple jump, the first two are still managed by the students.

Throwing: In the throwing world, Wen Jiufeng and Fan Guangwu, the two major North China shot putters, went to Germany and retired halfway (the so-called halfway retirement means giving up their athlete rights and not doing it, but occasionally they are happy to try it). Now, only Zhang Lingjia is trying it. Zhang was proficient in the three iron (shot put, discus, javelin), but due to the unfortunate fracture of his right arm, he gave up his promising javelin and did not do it. As for his heart, he still yearns for it. Zhang's discus can now be called a talent in China, and his decathlon is even more outstanding.

The Jiangsu Provincial Government is Planning to Block the Breach in the Canal

Using Soil from Zhenjiang Area

Regarding the blocking of the Jiangbei Canal Dike, it is said that the four places of Dangjun Building, Miaoxiangkou, Hehua Pond, and Zhaoguan Dam are the most important. However, according to experienced river workers, it is difficult to grab and block due to the inability to obtain soil. Later, after Jiangbei fellow villager Shen Zhuowu and Jiangsu Provincial Government Chairman Ye Chucang and others discussed, they hired Hua Engineering Engineer Zhuo Jing San and others and foreign engineers Gerk and others to inspect on the 10th of this month. After the inspection, a suitable method has been drafted. It will take about two months from the start of construction to complete the blocking. As for the soil collection, it is said that Shen Zhuowu has drafted a method and submitted it to Chairman Ye for approval. It is expected that a large amount of soil and stone will be transported from the soil mountains in Zhenjiang and Qixia Longtan and other places for application. Mr. Shen has come to Shanghai yesterday with Chinese and foreign engineers to rush to handle all the necessary items for transportation to Zhenjiang.

Yesterday's News on Disaster Relief in Various Provinces

Supervisory Committee Member Gao Yihan

Report on Inspection of Disaster Situation in Jiangbei

In order to understand the truth of the Jiangbei flood, the Supervisory Yuan specially sent Supervisory Committee member Gao Yihan to conduct an on-site inspection. He has now returned to Zhenjiang and will continue to inspect along the Jinghu Road. Yesterday, he sent a special letter to Xu Shiying, saying: Mr. Junren, I was ordered to inspect the flood situation in Jiangsu Province this time. I know that the disaster situation in Jiangbei is the most serious. Therefore, on the 3rd of this month, I first arrived in Zhenjiang. On the 4th, I went north from Guazhou, passing through Shaobo, Gaoyou, Baoying, Huai'an to Qingjiangpu. There are a total of 26 breaches along the way, with a total length of more than 800 zhang. Wherever the flood passed, the fields and houses were in ruins. The victims on both sides cried for help. The disaster situation in Gaoyou and Shaobo was especially tragic. Although the relief agencies and charitable organizations have released emergency relief, the disaster area is vast and there are many victims, making it difficult to reach everyone. During the visit along the dike, some people only have one meal a day, some only get one or two pieces of bread, and even some have nothing to eat all day long. Seeing this situation, it is difficult to continue. If funds are raised in the disaster area, the financial resources of each county are also insufficient. Woe to these survivors who do not die on the day the dike collapses, but die when the flood recedes. My heart is hurt and I am extremely worried. Therefore, when I returned to Shaobo, I sent a telegram on behalf of the victims to appeal to all parties for help, so that the victims in the disaster area would not be interrupted in their food supply. On the 8th, I went east from Shaobo along Xie Fenggang, intending to go to Xinghua by small steamer. When I passed Qiaoshu Town, I could not distinguish the river channel. The flood was vast and boundless. The water was five or six feet deep in the flat ground. The villages and houses were submerged, and there was no sign of human habitation in the wilderness. Even if there were residents, they were also sleeping in the open air between the dikes and on the trees. The remaining houses only had a few wooden pillars supporting a roof. The relief providers here were even rarer. As soon as they saw the small steamer passing by, they would steer small boats to carry the old and young to gather on the side of the steamer, crying for hunger and food. The small steamer I was on ran aground five or six times in the middle because it could not distinguish the waterway. Each time, there were four small boats gathering to beg us for relief. The more they gathered, the more they became. When I told them that this was a ship for inspecting the disaster, they all left with tears in their eyes. This situation cannot be fully depicted by even the drawings of refugees. On the morning of the 9th, I went to Taixian via the large culvert from Qiaoshu Town. I learned that the county was almost the same as Xinghua, and the disaster area reached more than two-thirds. I originally intended to go to Dongtai again, but I stopped because I could not distinguish the river channel along the way. According to the investigation, the counties of Xingtai and Dong were almost all lakes. The number of victims cannot be determined accurately, but if the relief funds do not arrive in a few days, I am afraid that the relief providers will only sit and wait for the victims to starve to death. Before arriving in the disaster area, I suspected that the disaster reports were exaggerated, but after experiencing it myself, I felt that the reports did not reach one in ten thousand of the actual situation. The cooked food transported from distant places is mostly rotten and inedible. However, if raw grain is transported, there is no dry firewood to cook it. If money is given for relief, there is no place to buy food. Seeing this situation, there is a strong desire to provide relief, but the inability to provide relief. What to do? The relief providers are worried every day that the relief supplies will not continue to arrive, making it difficult to cook without rice. I can only beg you to publicize the truth here to the charitable organizations at sea. The arrival of relief supplies one day earlier will save the lives of countless victims. I urgently express my words, and I respectfully wish you peace and health. Gao Yihan bowed and said on the 10th.

News from the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association

Disaster Situation in Xuzhou: The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association recently received a letter from Qiu Jun, a relief worker in Tongshan, saying that the disaster situation in Xuzhou is also very serious. The areas on both sides of Weishan Lake are the most serious. The miscellaneous grains such as beans, peanuts, and sesame have not been harvested at all. Even the sorghum harvested in the spring is less than 40% of the total harvest. In the past, when there were famines, the victims would flee to the south of the Yangtze River. This year, the disaster has spread across the country, and the victims have no way to escape. According to this situation, there will be 200,000 people who cannot live due to the disaster by winter. If it is not until the next spring, when the old grain is exhausted and the new grain is not yet available, the number will be even more unimaginable. The old and weak will turn to the ravines, and the strong will take risks. It is worrying everywhere. It is urgent to establish porridge factories and shelters. The association has now asked Qiao Mengqian to go to provide relief.

Relief Work in Yangzhou: Another telegram from the Yangzhou office said: Jiangsu Flood Relief Association, Yihan, Yisan, Jian, Mei Tongzhou and Xu Er brothers, Zhen, carried a large amount of relief supplies to the Gongdao Bridge and other places in Shui Ba Xiang to provide relief. After passing through more than 60 villages, no matter men, women, old or young, they all cried bitterly when they saw us. They used planks and leaned on trees for their homes. They had no clothes or blankets in the cold night. They suffered from dysentery and malaria. They were emaciated and haggard. All kinds of tragic situations made us want to cry without tears. On the way to You, we will return to Yangzhou tomorrow. Mei bowed, its behalf,

Two Letters Describing the Disaster in Xinghua

The Xinghua Fellow Villagers Association recently received two letters copied from Nantong, describing the heartbreaking and unbearable disaster in Xinghua. The contents are as follows: (1) To the two Zhang County Magistrates, Han, Uncle Yi County Magistrate, Cijian, I am grateful for your county's repeated dispatch of personnel to Xing to distribute emergency relief and rescue the refugees. Your kindness is immeasurable. Unfortunately, our county has suffered this great calamity. The disaster area covers an area of 7,200 square miles. The loss of fields, houses, and property is no less than 10,000,000 yuan. Corpses float along the river, and countless people have died. The surviving victims are climbing trees and roofs, urgently waiting to be rescued. In addition to the life-saving efforts of your county and the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association, according to reports, there are still tens of thousands of dying victims in the four villages who cannot survive. The situation is unbearable. We are currently telegraphing the provincial government to requisition a large number of ships and carry dry food for rapid relief. At the same time, we are asking various charitable organizations in China and abroad to immediately release relief funds to save lives. We still hope that the county magistrate and all legal groups will have compassion and consider the serious disaster situation in our county, widely publicize it, and find ways to provide relief. We are extremely grateful. Thank you specially. Respectfully wish you peace. Xinghua County Temporary Disaster Relief Association Standing Committee Shi Mingyong, Qi (2) To Nantong Fellow Villager Wang Jun, Letter, Xu Bai Mr. Jian, The current flood disaster in Xingyi is extremely tragic. Since the breaches in You and Shao, the water level has suddenly increased by several feet. The deep ones are more than a zhang, and the shallow ones are up to the knees. The city and the countryside are the same. It is impossible to find a few square feet of dry land to live in. The houses along the river outside the city are all collapsing due to the impact of the wind and waves. It is shocking to see, such as the Dawang Temple, Prajna Nunnery, Guanyin Pavilion, Chenghuang Xing Palace, Yeguandi Temple, Zhunti Nunnery, etc. outside the north city, all of which are solid and tall houses, and almost all of them have been demolished. Others can be imagined. In the countryside, no matter where the houses are, they have all been swept away by the water. Not only are furniture and property lost, but also food has been washed away. There are people who are drowned, starved to death, and desperately seeking death everywhere. The exact number is still unknown. Such a great calamity has never been heard of in ancient times. We are temporarily in local positions and try our best to fulfill our responsibilities. I really don't know where to start. I am very grateful to the disaster relief team of your county for bringing a large amount of relief supplies and distributing them. Mr. Mang also took 250 victims back to Tong to accommodate them. I am especially grateful to County Magistrate Zhang and the local legal groups for their kindness in saving lives thoroughly. Please trouble Mr. Quan to thank them all on my behalf. However, the land is vast, the victims are numerous, and the future is long. The water has not yet receded, and the people's livelihood has no chance of turning around. The dead before and after are afraid that they will still not be spared. Every time I think about it, I can only cry bitterly. The tragic situation of the disaster is beyond description. I briefly describe a few lines, hoping that you will understand. I wish you a safe journey. Your brother Gu Lunan, Qi, September 7th (Gu is the chairman of the Xinghua Chamber of Commerce.)

Cao Deliang Talks About the Disaster Situation in Taixian

Cao Deliang, chairman of the Taixian Chamber of Commerce, came to Shanghai on business. According to his words yesterday, it rained heavily in Taixian in July. The southeast and southwest areas are originally high in terrain. Due to the continuous heavy rain, the water stagnated and was difficult to recede, and there were signs of being flooded. The northern villages are all paddy fields, so even if there is a little more rainfall, it will not be a big problem. However, people's hearts are already uneasy. At the beginning of August, the Cheluo Wuli Xinba Sanba opened at the same time, and the west water flowed down. The water level in the lower river rose sharply, and most of the northern villages were flooded. The people in the Xiefenggang area were already flooded in their homes, so they gathered to live on the dikes. Unexpectedly, a sudden storm arose, drumming up the raging waves. The Xiedi, which was known to be solid, suddenly collapsed. The people who were living on the dike were unable to escape and were all swept into the flood by the huge waves. The number of deaths could not be counted. When the breaches in Gao and Shao occurred, Taixian rose by three feet again. The deepest place was more than the top of the head, and the shallowest place was also two or three feet. The four districts of Gangzi, Fanchuan, Bantun, and Xiaoji were completely submerged in the water. The Taicheng originally had a disaster prevention committee, but it was reorganized into a flood relief committee and quickly carried out relief. They hired small steamships to go to the villages to rescue the victims. At the same time, private philanthropists also hired ships to rescue them. However, the disaster area was too wide, making it difficult to rescue everyone from the water. As for the collapse of houses and the snatching of rice, which was washed away and no longer existed, it should be the meaning in the topic. Now, the work of the relief committee members is extremely intense. Under the committee, there are ten groups: general affairs, accounting, condolences, supervision, life-saving, transportation, health, accommodation of victims, purchase of farming cattle, and food management, each with one person responsible for presiding over. I am in charge of the work of the accommodation of victims group, with a total of ten shelters, with 5,000 victims. The victims from Xinghua, Dongtai, and other villages in our county are still coming in an endless stream. Limited by funding, it is not easy to accommodate them all. At present, the water level has not receded slightly. Two-thirds of the county's land is submerged in water. There are at least 200,000 victims struggling in the water waiting to die. Those in the shallower places can barely survive. There are hundreds of thousands of victims waiting for relief. The urban area is high, and fortunately, it has not been completely submerged. However, the basket shop outside the north gate has water up to the ankles, gradually deepening to the north. Looking north from the end of the city, it is a vast expanse of water. Those who go to inspect only see that the most prosperous area of Pozi Street has not changed its old appearance, and think that the disaster situation in Taixian is not serious, which is a big mistake. Cao also talked about relief, saying that two-thirds of the land in Taixian is submerged, and there are the most serious and tragic four districts of Gangzi, Potun, Fanchuan, and Xiaoji. There are too many victims, and it is impossible to provide relief with the tens of thousands of yuan raised locally. Even with 200,000 victims waiting to die, each person would need one yuan, which would require 200,000 yuan. Ask what good is it to give each person one yuan? Therefore, the provincial government must have concrete measures and a large amount of relief funds, and must conduct a careful investigation and distribute them on the ground before it can be effective. Moreover, the already breached breach has not been blocked, and the old course to the sea cannot be smoothly discharged. If Gao and Shao recede by one point, then Tai, Xing, and Dong will increase by one point. Although the disaster situation in Gao and Shao is serious, the water will pass quickly, while Taixian will be forever submerged in the vast water, and it is unknown when it will be able to escape the disaster.

Shanghai County Government Encourages the Donation of Old Clothes for Victims

The Shanghai County Government yesterday issued an order to the county's various agencies, saying: According to the document and telegram from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, this year, the disaster-stricken area of this province has reached almost nine-tenths, and the counties along the canal are especially tragic. Regarding the accommodation and relief, this government has been actively preparing and implementing it in order. However, it is the time of late autumn, and the severe cold is approaching. The item of clothing for the victims should also be prepared in advance. In addition to sending separate telegrams to the Commander-in-Chief and ordering the Civil Affairs Department and the Security Department to quickly allocate broken and old clothes used by the military police to this government for transfer and assistance, it is necessary to send a telegram to the county magistrate to quickly announce to all sectors that anyone who has stored old clothes for men and women, whether men, women, old or young, single cotton, silk, or cloth, should donate as much as possible. Hand them over to the county government for transfer to the relief association for distribution. Also, immediately gather the heads of the districts, villages, and towns and their deputies to be responsible for encouraging donations, so that the victims can obtain tools to keep out the cold. The time is urgent, and there should be no delay. It is important, etc. Upon receiving this, it was submitted for discussion at the 73rd county political meeting on the 14th of this month, and it was decided to issue a notice to all agencies to collect old clothes within ten days and hand them over to the county for transfer, etc. In addition to complying with the notice and sending it to the departments, it is also ordered to comply with it, quickly collect old clothes for men and women, and hand them over to the county within ten days for collection and transfer. It concerns the relief of the victims, the time is urgent, and there should be no delay. It is important.

Disaster Relief Work of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association

Rushing to Make Cotton Clothes: The association, in view of the increasing cold weather and the victims without clothes, is rushing to make 30,000 sets of cotton clothes for distribution. However, local coarse cloth is no longer available for purchase. It has specially ordered it from Nantong Tiansheng No. 1 Factory. It will be shipped out soon. However, the cost of new clothes is more expensive, and it is still difficult to meet the urgent needs. If all sectors have old clothes and quilts, rather than storing them in the attic and occupying space, why not donate them to the victims, so that they can create infinite blessings?

Shipping out Flour: The 10,000 bags of flour purchased by the association for the Yangzhou branch have been loaded by the Datong Shipping Company and are allowed to be shipped out today. The company has also agreed to load them for free.

Overseas Chinese Donations: The association received 10,000 yuan remitted from the San Francisco Chinese Association and the Chinese Chamber of Commerce to donate to the Southeast flood disaster relief. The Guangdong Bank of New York remitted 13,122 yuan donated by eight overseas Chinese families.

Public Group Donations: The association received 2,000 yuan donated by the members of the Shanghai Hardware Industry Association for the flood disaster. In addition, individuals who came to the association to donate were also quite enthusiastic. The names are too many to be recorded.

Continued Report from the Red Cross Hankou Relief Team

The Chinese Red Cross Society yesterday received a report from the Hankou relief team it sent, saying that it had been working in the Heshan area of Hanyang for several days, treating about 2,000 victims, most of whom were suffering from dysentery and malaria. They worked from 8:00 am to 4:00 pm and treated an average of about 1,000 victims per day. There are also 47 shelters set up in Hanyang, Wuchang, and Hankou, with about 100,000 victims, who are also in urgent need of medical treatment. Therefore, they have been extremely busy these days. The water level has not yet receded and there is a risk of continued flooding. Transportation is difficult. Fortunately, the Hankou branch hired rowing boats, which was very convenient. The disaster area films have been shot and will be sent soon. However, the disaster area is vast and there are many victims, and the medicines they brought are not enough. Please find a way to send more medicines to save the victims. After receiving the report, the association has replied by telegram that it will successively send more medicines within a few days to provide assistance.

The Guangzhao Association Sends Cantonese Fellow Villagers Affected by the Disaster Back to Their Hometowns

The Guangzhao Association and the Cantonese Commercial Federation, in view of the large number of Cantonese people in Wuhan who have been affected by the disaster, sent people to Wuhan a month ago with funds to provide on-site relief, summoned the Cantonese people affected by the disaster to come to Shanghai in batches, and provided them with funds to return to their hometowns. Yesterday, Chen Bingqian, a director of the association, personally went to Mingli Inn to offer condolences. He then discussed the repatriation method with Zheng Jianzhi, the manager of the inn, and hired famous doctors to inject anti-dysentery vaccines for the refugees. Currently, the first batch of more than 70 refugees will take the Suiyang transport ship back to Guangdong today. Along the way, Mingli Inn will send additional helpers to take care of them.

Recent Situation of Emergency Relief in Various Provinces

Hubei Province: The Emergency Relief Association has remitted a total of 65,000 yuan for disaster relief. Li, the head of the training corps, has already organized two teams to provide relief in severely affected areas. The first team is heading to Xindi, and the second team to Fankou, both carrying relief supplies and funds, and have departed separately.

Anhui Province: Various relief associations have allocated a total of 127,000 yuan for Anhui disaster relief. The funds have been entrusted to Liu Lingsheng, Xu Pingxuan, Zhai Zhancheng, Zhang Rujun, and others for distribution. Of Luo Jialing's 20,000 yuan, 10,000 yuan is earmarked for retrieving and burying corpses, entrusted to Zhang Rujun who will organize a team from the Wuhu Flood Relief Association to depart. Another 10,000 yuan is allocated for emergency relief in Langxi, Guichi, Tongling, Dongliu, and Qiupu, entrusted to the Red Swastika Society to travel separately, coordinate with local authorities, and conduct thorough investigations for distribution. Moreover, the disaster is severe in Fan and Tu counties, and relief workers have telegraphed for emergency assistance. The China Bank remitted 10,000 yuan from the Shanghai Flood Relief Association to distribute on the 11th.

Jiangsu Province: The Emergency Relief Association telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government regarding the disaster area north of the Yangtze River, urging immediate action to block breaches, reduce river water levels, and provide hope for wheat planting. It also entrusted Committee Member Zhang to go to Zhenjiang to discuss breach plugging, requesting the Provincial Government to send technical personnel along. Another telegram was sent to Leng Yuqiu urging quick breach plugging, inquiring about the quantity of required materials such as stone strips, willow branches, bamboo stakes, lead wire, six-inch large nails, ropes, and麻袋 (gunny sacks), whether they are easily available locally, or if any are already prepared, requesting detailed information for advance preparation.

Jiangxi Province: Jiujiang Special Commissioner Zhou Peng telegraphed the Emergency Relief Association, stating that Jiujiang has a large number of disaster victims. They are considering two approaches: providing congee to over 16,000 elderly and weak individuals and relocating over 10,000 able-bodied men. 20,000 yuan has been remitted to establish shelters. Furthermore, the Jiangxi Provincial Chamber of Commerce Joint Association telegraphed, stating that the disaster-stricken area in Jiangxi Province covers 3,700 square miles, with extremely dire conditions.

Henan Province: The Henan Province Flood Relief Association telegraphed that 67 counties in Henan Province have been affected by floods, with 15 million disaster victims in urgent need of relief. The Emergency Relief Association has telegraphed Committee Member Wang Pinggeng to inquire about the amount of funds needed. Relief measures will be determined upon receiving a reply.

Hunan Province: The Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee telegraphed that over 60 counties in the province are disaster areas, with over 12 million disaster victims. The Emergency Relief Association has dispatched Committee Member Zhao Shouyu from Shanghai to Hankou and then to Hunan to inspect and plan the work.

Zhejiang Province: The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Civil Affairs Relief Association telegraphed that dikes and embankments in Yuqian, Yuhang, Hangzhou, Wukang, Deqing, Wuxing, Changxing, Anji, and Xiaofeng have collapsed, and fields have been damaged. Yuhang, Wukang, Wuxing, and Changxing are particularly severely affected. In Chongde, Haiyan, Jiaxing, and Jiashan, a significant amount of farmland has been flooded. Fuyang and Xiaoshan have also been severely affected. In Chun'an, a large amount of miscellaneous grain farmland has been washed away. In Dinghai, Fenghua, Zhenhai, Shaoxian, Xiaoshan, Shaoxing, Shengxian, Yiwu, Dongyang, and Zhuji, dikes and embankments have collapsed, houses have been blown down, and crops have been completely submerged. Jinyun and Jinhua have been affected by hurricanes.

Shandong Province: Han Fuqu telegraphed that over ten counties, including Yixian, Dingtao, Ziyang, and Licheng, have been hit by floods. The number of counties reporting disasters has reached thirty, and the river water is still rising.

Fujian Province: Yang Shuzhuang telegraphed that continuous rain has caused disasters in Sha County, Dehua, Xiaoqing, and other counties. A typhoon in Funing has resulted in over a thousand deaths, the collapse of over 20,000 houses, and the sinking of over a thousand ships, affecting hundreds of thousands of disaster victims. The typhoon disasters are particularly severe in Fuzhou, Zhangzhou, and their subordinate areas, especially in the coastal counties of eastern Fujian. The counties that have reported disasters include Liancheng, Ningyang, Yong'an, Minhou, Xiapu, Fuding, Gutian, Lianjiang, Luoyuan, Longxi, Zhangpu, Yi'an, Yunxiao, and others.

Shaanxi Province: The Baoguang Industrial Xingqiao Construction Office reported that due to heavy rain, the river water surged to a height of 20 feet and a width of over 40 feet, destroying the bridge. Due to the overwhelming force of the water, rescue efforts were impossible.

Gansu Province: The Provincial Relief Association telegraphed that a surge of water occurred in Gaolan and Hubei Township. Torrential rain and flash floods, accompanied by hail, occurred in Pengjiadun, Shili Store, and other places, washing away over 550 acres of farmland and damaging the automotive engineering projects. In Haojiaying, Yuzhong, and other places, heavy hail fell on the same day, damaging autumn crops and destroying any chance of harvest.

Yunnan Province: Long Yun telegraphed that rising water and collapsing embankments have caused disasters in Yanzhou, Zhaotong, Yiliang, and other three counties.

Qinghai Province: The Provincial Relief Association reported that Qinghai Province experienced severe drought in the spring, followed by heavy rain in the summer, along with hail and sudden violent winds. Grain losses in Xining, Huangyuan, Huzhu, Ledu, Bayan, Datong, Xunhua, Guide, and other counties have been total. Numerous corpses are floating along the rivers. The disaster-stricken area accounts for 60-70% of the entire province.
